I can't believe it&rsquo;s practically the end of summer. All the shows we've been working on for The Grand Ballroom at Webster Hall (you may know it as the "Main Room") are rapidly approaching. With this new chapter of concert bookings in The Grand Ballroom, comes a new sound system.

 A total of 50 new L-Acoustics Kara speakers & subwoofers for our customers (you!) plus 25 monitors & subwoofers for the stage (for the band!) along with DigiCo mixing consoles are now installed. That means we will have a much higher level of audio quality along with better coverage (you'll hear clearer music, without it being painfully loud in the front row!) Come to a show and take a listen.

We're here to provide the best concert and nightlife experience possible - and your feedback and suggestions are always welcomed. Are you ready? We are.
